***blitz.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:blitz.html>blitz</a> (14576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortened <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:blitzkrieg.html>blitzkrieg</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:blitzkrieg.html>Blitzkrieg</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
